<text>Converted auto body shop turned into one of the hottest ticket in town. Hip, airy, buzzing, urban vibe with great views over Divisadero.

Able to get seats right away at 6pm on Friday at the bar. Had to wait a bit for drinks and food but everything was good if not mind-blowing. Bartender wisely suggested half orders of pasta when we (2 of us) tried to order salad, 2 pastas AND pizza üê∑

Pizza thicker/more doughy and a lot smaller than Ragazza/Gialina. Classic climbing in San Diego.  A.k.a. "the grunge" one can expect to find footwork difficult to get at first.  But if you can learn to smear at rhe gorge, then your gonna be able to smear anywhere.  I recommend doing Suzies Wild Ride, Hangmans Climb, Escapade, Quantum Leap, Dark Rider and General Dynamics.  For those looking for a real challenge there is the Thumb, I wish you luck on that beast!</Review>

<rate>4</rate>< Text>
Great authentic Colombian food, very meaty and savory. They have lots of colombian packaged candy and sodas for sale to take home. The juices are also amazing they have passion fruit, guava, blackberry and more, so good and fresh.  Also the empanadas are so good and crispy not like some other places with soggy ones they make a great side to whatever meal you get. They come in beef , chicken and cheese. When coming just know that everything is made to order so it will take longer than a regular restaurant. Good restaurant not the best I've ever had but better than average. Also the colombiana soda is like a regular coke but with a bubblegum after taste weird but really good.</Text>

<Review>Where do I begin? This place is beautiful.  We went while there was still snow capping the mountains so the views were out of this world.  First, the drive to the lake is beautiful.  The closer you get,  the more scenic it becomes.  Once you get there,  the colors of nature explode.  The lake wasn't just blue,  it was a vibrate turquoise. The air was clean and crisp.  The sound if the lake opening to a stream was peaceful.

We rented a boat and stayed out on the lake for a few hours. The customer service was awesome.  Those guys went above and beyond.  Overall,  I'd highly recommend this lake.</Review>< resp>

<review>I was here on October/25/20.
Convict lake is one of the most beautiful and easy to access.
The lake has campground, fishing and hiking trail, all with a stunning backdrop.
It is 2.5 miles hiking loop, not much of elevation gain.
I did not hike around it so I cannot comment on the trail,but I can imagine it is worth to doing it for stunning views.
It is one of the most spectacular fall colors, the best show of glowing golden- orange- crimson fall colors in western United States.
The water as clear as glass and the reflection of mountains surrounding around convict lake are breathtaking as well.
This is the best  place to take beautiful fall colors  pictures.< /review>< Pics>

< username>
John P< /username>
<date>1603253441197<//date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
I visited convict lake in the wrong day. Due to Creek wild fire, the air quality is absolute miserable. AQI is over 300. A smog blanketed the whole area around mammoth lakes. All in all, convict lake is still as beautiful and busy as usual. Tons of visitors ignored the smog and enjoyed their time with the fishing, boating, and photographing.

Convict lake is about 15 minutes driving from mammoth lakes. Mount Morison and Laurel and Bloody Mountains circles around the lake and Aspen trees along the shore shows pretty reflection in the lake. If you ever wonder where all the mountain's name comes from. You shall know the incident happened around this lake over a hundred years ago. On 10/17/1871, 29 convicts broke out of a prison in Carson City. Some of them fled to this area to hide and eventually died at this lake. A shootout occured on that day, a few prisoners were wound and two locals were killed. Since then, Convict Lake got its name from this incident. Mt. Morrison and Mono Jim Peak were named after the two killed locals. Of course, you know why there is a bloody mountain by the lake.

There is an easy 2.5 mile hiking trail loop around the lake. The total elevation is about 180 feets. For the best view, you shall hike around the lake anti-clockwise. You can park either at the convict lake trail head  near fistherman's trail, or at the convict lake marina. Both places have lot of parking slots. There are plenty vista points around the lake, and lake shore is quite easy to access from the trail.<//Text>

Bob Thompson</name>
< time>
1615476526898</time>
<Rate>4<//Rate><review>Roughly 2 miles up a windy road, off of         Highway 395, lies Convict Lake, named after a band of outlaws who hid out up here, long ago.

At an elevation of 7,850 ft., strenuous hikes around the lake will take your breath away.  When visiting most of these high altitude Sierra lakes, first light is the best time to fish, as well as do photography.  You can catch rainbow trout & brown trout in this regularly stocked lake.  In the early morning hours, when the wind hasn't kicked up yet, you can capture some really nice mirror-like reflection pics of the lake.

Convict Lake resembles a huge bowl.  The barren Sierra peaks act as the sides of the bowl.  You'll see bushes & trees around the lake, but the majority of Convict Lake's surroundings are as sheer & rocky as a Martian landscape.

Last time I was here, in June 2016, I saw 2 young Mule Deer in the parking lot, right after getting out of the car.  They weren't the least bit fearful of me, as they made their way to some nearby bushes, and lazily grazed on vegetation.

I caught one rainbow trout here that time, a nice 2lb. specimen, which I BBQ'd later that day, using lots of butter, salt & pepper, fresh herbs and sliced almonds.  The larger trout are easier to eat than the smaller ones, since the larger trout's bones come out more easily, all in one piece, when the fish is perfectly cooked.

My wife and I saw a Bald Eagle at Convict Lake, first soaring, then perched way up high in a tall Pine tree.

Convict Lake is a fairly good fishing spot, featuring stark, rugged natural beauty.</review>< Pictures>
None<//Pictures>

< username>
Claudia S.< /username>
<Date>1512921465392< /Date>< Rate>
5< /Rate>
< text>
Absolutely beautiful place. The water is crystal clear. If you are brave, go for a swim (it gets better after 20-30 seconds in the water). The fishermen are a little touchy and bossy about "scaring the fish." But the shoreline is full of tangles of fishing line, a danger to all the wildlife that lives there. If you have time, like I did, pick up all the tangles of fishing line that you see and throw it in the garbage cans. The campground sites are small and really close to each other, and $25! I had a neighbor with 2 vehicles (from Florida) that returned to their site at 2am in the morning, and started making a fire, flashing car lights and overall unprepared for a freezing night. I got beautiful photos, but I don't plan on camping here again (would like to try one of the cabins though). Haven't eaten at the restaurants, but my parents did and wouldn't stop raving about how good it was.</text>

<Text>Crystal clear (and cold) waters. Some rental boats but otherwise calm and relaxing. There's a public trail all around the lake and spots every 100 feet or so that go down to the water where you can hangout/picnic/etc. Nearby are bathrooms and parking lots as well as campgrounds. Dogs welcome on leash. Show up early (before 10am) if you want the "best" spots and parking. I've seen some people pull some massive trout from this lake right from shore.<//Text><Pics>None< /Pics></record></dataset><record>

<name>Monica Sierra</name><date>1552836286927<//date><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>This is one of my favorite places in the world.  This lake is as clear as glass, full of fish and has exceptionally stunning beauty!  All of the lakes in Mammoth are pristine but Convict Lake has amazing beauty.  The water has that turquoise color that comes from the minerals of melting glaciers and it is super clear.  My favorite time there is fall as I LOVE the magnificent colors.  It is great for hiking, fishing, boat rentals are avaliable, there is a restaurant about 3 minutes away from the water, small cabins to rent and horses for rent at certa8n times of the year.  My photos are from fall and my favorites.  I plan to visit every year.< /Review>< pictures>

I was like what the hell is this! Since when are people allowed to snorkel in the lake? Well that just ruined my fishing in that spot! I sit there for 3 more hours with not a single bite! I went back out later in the evening to the south shore only to get there and people had their dogs swimming in the lake! At that point I just said forget it and went back to camp!
